-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "STRESS_WORK",
                "NAME": "Stress at Work Questionnaire",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale of 1-10, how stressed do you feel at work?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "1"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "2"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "3"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "4"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "5"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "6"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "7"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "8"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER":"9"
                             },
                             { 
                                 
                                 
                                 
                                 
                                 
                                 
                                 
                                
                               }
                              ]
                    },
                    {
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                           {"ANSWER":"Yes"},
                           {"ANSWER":"No"}
                        ],
                        "_TF_QUESTIONS":[
                           {"CODE":"Q2",
                           "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                              {"ANSWER":"Yes"},
                              {"ANSWER":"No"}
                           ],
                           "_TF_QUESTIONS":[],
                           }
                           
                           
                           
                           
                           
                           
                           
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                        ],
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                    }
                ]
            }
        ]
    }
}

If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

-------------------

          {
            "CODE": "WE_Q01_01",

					"ANSWER":"Yes, it is perfect."
				},
				{
					"ANSWER":"It could be better."
				},

  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.

Generate me a questionnaire on Remote working experience
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "RWEXP001",
                "NAME": "Remote Working Experience Questionnaire",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale of 1 to 10, how comfortable are you with remote working?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER":"1"},

                            {"ANSWER":"10"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q2",
                        "NAME": "How often do you feel isolated while working remotely?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 1,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER":"Never"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Rarely"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Sometimes"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Often"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q3",
                        "NAME": "What is your preferred method of communication while working remotely?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 2,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                          { 
                              'ANSWER': 'Email'
                          },
                          { 
                              'ANSWER': 'Instant Messaging'
                          },
                          { 
                              'ANSWER': 'Video Conferencing'
                          },
                          { 
                              'ANSWER': 'Phone Calls'
                          }
                      ]
                    },
                    {
                      'CODE':'Q4',
                      'NAME':'Do you have a dedicated workspace at home?',
                      'TYPE_ID':1,
                      'DISPLAY_ORDER':4,
                      '_TF_ANSWERS':[
                          {'ANSWER':'Yes'},
                          {'ANSWER':'No'}
                      ]
                  },
                  {
                      'CODE':'Q5',

                  }

Generate me a questionnaire on End of working relationship
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "EOWR_Q",
                "NAME": "End of Working Relationship Questionnaire",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale of 1 to 10, how satisfied were you with your overall experience working with us?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER":"1"},
                            {"ANSWER":"2"},
                            {"ANSWER":"3"},

                            {"ANSWER":"9"},
                            {"ANSWER":"10"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q2",
                        "NAME": "What was the reason for your departure?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 2,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                            {"ANSWER":"Better opportunity elsewhere."},
                            {"ANSWER":"Personal reasons."},
                            {"ANSWER":"Disagreement with management."},
                            {"ANSWER":"Lack of growth opportunities."},
                            {"ANSWER":"Unsatisfactory compensation and benefits."},
                            {"ANSWER":"Other (please specify):"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q3",
                        "NAME": "Did you feel that your contributions were valued by the company?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 1,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                          { 
                              'CODE': 'A',
                              'NAME': 'Yes'
                          },
                          { 
                              'CODE': 'B',
                              'NAME': 'No'
                          }
                      ]
                    },
                    {
                      'CODE': 'Q4',
                      'NAME': 'How would you rate the support provided by HR during your exit process?',
                      'TYPE_ID': 3,
                      'DISPLAY_ORDER': 4,
                      '_TF_ANSWERS':[ 
                          {'ANSWER':'1'},
                          {'ANSWER':'2'},
                          {'ANSWER':'3'},
                          {'ANSWER':'4'},
                          {'ANSWER':'5'},
                          {'ANSWER':'6'},
                          {'ANSWER':'7'},
                          {'ANSWER':'8'},
                          {'ANSWER':'9'},
                          {'ANSWER':'10'}
                      ]
                  },
                  {
                      'CODE': 'Q5',
                      'NAME': 'Would you recommend our company to others as a good place to work?',
                      'TYPE_ID': 1,
                      'DISPLAY_ORDER': 5,
                      '_TF_ANSWERS':[ 
                         { 
                             'CODE': 'A',
                             'NAME': 'Yes'
                         },
                         { 
                             'CODE': 'B',
                             NAME:   No
                         }
                     ]
                  }
                ]
            }

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1173005
     - Topic: Employee feedback
     - Question number: 4
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Employee feedback
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "EMP_FEEDBACK_001",
        "NAME": "Employee Feedback Questionnaire",

        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q001",
            "NAME": "On a scale of 1 to 5, how satisfied are you with your job?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "1"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "2"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "3"

              },
              {

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500000003
     - Topic: Employee potential
     - Question number: 8
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Employee potential
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "EMP_POTENTIAL",
                "NAME": "Employee Potential Questionnaire",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale of 1 to 10, how would you rate the employee's ability to learn new skills?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": []
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q2",
                        "NAME": "How often does the employee take initiative in their work?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 1,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER":"Rarely"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Sometimes"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Often"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Almost always"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q3",
                        "NAME": "Does the employee have good problem-solving skills?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                            {"ANSWER":"Yes"},
                            {"ANSWER":"No"}
                         ],
                         DISPLAY_ORDER: 3
                    },
                    {
                     	"CODE":"Q4",
                     	"NAME":"How would you rate the employee's communication skills?",
                     	"TYPE_ID":3,
                     	"DISPLAY_ORDER":4,
                     	"_TF_ANSWERS":[]
                   },
                   {
                     	"CODE":"Q5",
                     	"NAME":"Does the employee work well in a team environment?",
                     	"TYPE_ID":2,
                     	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                         {"ANSWER":"Yes"},
                         {"ANSWER":"No"}
                       ],
                       DISPLAY_ORDER:5
                   }
                ]
            }
        ]
    }
}

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User:

-------------------

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100012
     - Topic: Employee motivation
     - Question number: 5
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Employee motivation
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "EMP_MOT_001",
                "NAME": "Employee Motivation Questionnaire",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale of 1-10, how motivated are you to come to work every day?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {"ANSWER":"1"},
                            {"ANSWER":"2"},
                            {"ANSWER":"3"},
                            {"ANSWER":"4"},
                            {"ANSWER":"5"},
                            {"ANSWER":"6"},
                            {"ANSWER":"7"},
                            {"ANSWER":"8"},
                            {"ANSWER":"9"},
                            {"ANSWER":"10"}
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q2",
                        "NAME": "What motivates you the most at work?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 2,

        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.

  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Kick-off Meeting Feedback
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "KM_FEEDBACK",
                "NAME": "Kick-off Meeting Feedback",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "How satisfied are you with the overall organization of the kick-off meeting?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS": [
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "Very Satisfied"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "Satisfied"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "Neutral"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "Dissatisfied"
                            },
                            {
                                "ANSWER": "Very Dissatisfied"
                            }
                        ]
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q2",
                        "NAME": "Did the kick-off meeting meet your expectations?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 1,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                          {
                              'ANSWER': 'Yes'
                          },
                          {
                              'ANSWER': 'No'
                          }
                      ],
                      'DISPLAY_ORDER': 2
                    },
                    {
                      'CODE': 'Q3',
                      'NAME': 'What did you like most about the kick-off meeting?',
                      'TYPE_ID': 4,
                      '_TF_ANSWERS': [],
                      'DISPLAY_ORDER': 3
                    },
                    {
                      'CODE': 'Q4',
                      'NAME': 'What did you like least about the kick-off meeting?',
                      'TYPE_ID': 4,

            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Recognition and Rewards
-------------------
-------------------

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User:

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100051
     - Topic: Work-Life Balance
     - Question number: 6
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Work-Life Balance
-------------------
-------------------

If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User:

        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment
